<Silverscreen> 1,11RANDOM MOVIE TRIVIA: Phoebus' anthropomorphic horse is named Achilles. The name gives two jokes. At one point, Phoebus commands, "Achilles, sit!" - and the horse promptly sits down. first, it assumes (correctly, in this case) that the war horse will obey a command normally used for a trained dog. Second, the line is a pun on the phrase "Achilles' heel", a term for a person's weakness
<Polydunami> Reboot, Ghosties
<Silverscreen> 1,11(which itself derives from Achilles in Greek mythology, who was invulnerable except for one heel; the Achilles tendon in the ankle is also named for this).
